title="Air purifier">\n        Air purifier \xc2\xa7\xc2\xa0Potential ozone hazards\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Devices generating high levels of ozone, some of which use ionization, are used to sanitize and deodorize uninhabited buildings, rooms, ductwork, woodsheds, boats and other vehicles.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In the U.S.,\n       <a href="/wiki/Air_purifier" title="Air purifier">\n        air purifiers\n       </a>\n       emitting low levels of ozone have been sold. This kind of air purifier is sometimes claimed to imitate nature\'s way of purifying the air without filters and to sanitize both it and household surfaces. The\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Environmental_Protection_Agency" title="United States Environmental Protection Agency">\n        United States Environmental Protection Agency\n       </a>\n       (EPA) has declared that there is "evidence to show that at concentrations that do not exceed public health standards, ozone is not effective at removing many odor-causing chemicals" or "viruses, bacteria, mold, or other biological pollutants". Furthermore, its report states that "results of some controlled studies show that concentrations of ozone considerably higher than these [human safety] standards are possible even when a user follows the manufacturer\xe2\x80\x99s operating instructions".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-93">\n        <a href="#cite_note-93">\n         [92]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Ozonated water is used to launder clothes and to sanitize food, drinking water, and surfaces in the home. According to the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._Food_and_Drug_Administration" title="U.S. Food and Drug Administration">\n        U.S. Food and Drug Administration\n       </a>\n       (FDA), it is "amending the\n       <a href="/wiki/Food_additive" title="Food additive">\n        food additive\n       </a>\n       regulations to provide for the safe use of ozone in gaseous and aqueous phases as an\n       <a href="/wiki/Antimicrobial" title="Antimicrobial">\n        antimicrobial agent\n       </a>\n       on food, including meat and poultry." Studies at\n       <a href="/wiki/California_Polytechnic_State_University" title="California Polytechnic State University">\n        California Polytechnic University\n       </a>\n       demonstrated that 0.3 \xce\xbcmol/mol levels of ozone dissolved in filtered tapwater can produce a reduction of more than 99.99% in such food-borne microorganisms as salmonella,\n       <i>\n        E. coli\n       </i>\n       0157:H7 and\n       <i>\n        Campylobacter\n       </i>\n       . This quantity is 20,000 times the\n       <a href="/wiki/World_Health_Organization" title="World Health Organization">\n        WHO\n       </a>\n       -recommended limits stated above.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-food_86-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-food-86">\n         [85]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-94">\n        <a href="#cite_note-94">\n         [93]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Ozone can be used to remove\n       <a href="/wiki/Pesticide" title="Pesticide">\n        pesticide\n       </a>\n       residues from\n       <a href="/wiki/Fruit" title="Fruit">\n        fruits\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Vegetable" title="Vegetable">\n        vegetables\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-95">\n        <a href="#cite_note-95">\n         [94]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fruit_96-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fruit-96">\n         [95]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Ozone is used in homes and\n       <a href="/wiki/Hot_tub" title="Hot tub">\n        hot tubs\n       </a>\n       to kill bacteria in the water and to reduce the amount of chlorine or bromine required by reactivating them to their free state. Since ozone does not remain in the water long enough, ozone by itself is ineffective at preventing cross-contamination among bathers and must be used in conjunction with\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Halogens" title="Halogens">\n        halogens\n       </a>\n       . Gaseous ozone created by ultraviolet light or by corona discharge is injected into the water.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-97">\n        <a href="#cite_note-97">\n         [96]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Ozone is also widely used in treatment of water in aquariums and fish ponds. Its use can minimize bacterial growth, control parasites, eliminate transmission of some diseases, and reduce or eliminate "yellowing" of the water. Ozone must not come in contact with fish\'s gill structures. Natural salt water (with life forms) provides enough "instantaneous demand" that controlled amounts of ozone activate bromide ion to\n       <a href="/wiki/Hypobromous_acid" title="Hypobromous acid">\n        hypobromous acid\n       </a>\n       , and the ozone entirely decays in a few seconds to minutes. If oxygen fed ozone is used, the water will be higher in dissolved oxygen, fish\'s gill structures will atrophy and they will become dependent on higher dissolved oxygen levels.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Aquaculture">\n        Aquaculture\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Ozone&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Aquaculture">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Ozonation \xe2\x80\x93 a process of infusing water with ozone \xe2\x80\x93 can be used in aquaculture to facilitate organic breakdown. Ozone is also added to recirculating systems to reduce\n       <a href="/wiki/Nitrite" title="Nitrite">\n        nitrite\n       </a>\n       levels\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Noble_98-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Noble-98">\n         [97]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       through conversion into\n       <a href="/wiki/Nitrate" title="Nitrate">\n        nitrate\n       </a>\n       . If nitrite levels in the water are high, nitrites will also accumulate in the blood and tissues of fish, where it interferes with oxygen transport (it causes oxidation of the heme-group of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Haemoglobin" title="Haemoglobin">\n        haemoglobin\n       </a>\n       from ferrous (\n       <span class="chemf nowrap">\n        Fe\n        <span style="display:inline-block;margin-bottom:-0.3em;vertical-align:0.8em;line-height:1em;font-size:80%;text-align:left">\n         2+\n         <br/>\n        </span>\n       </span>\n       ) to ferric (\n       <span class="chemf nowrap">\n        Fe\n        <span style="display:inline-block;margin-bottom:-0.3em;vertical-align:0.8em;line-height:1em;font-size:80%;text-align:left">\n         3+\n         <br/>\n        </span>\n       </span>\n       ), making haemoglobin unable to bind\n       <span class="chemf nowrap">\n        O\n        <span style="display:inline-block;margin-bottom:-0.3em;vertical-align:-0.4em;line-height:1em;font-size:80%;text-align:left">\n         <br/>\n         2\n        </span>\n       </span>\n       ).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ferreira_99-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Ferreira-99">\n         [98]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Despite these apparent positive effects, ozone use in recirculation systems has been linked to reducing the level of bioavailable iodine in salt water systems, resulting in iodine deficiency symptoms such as goitre and decreased growth in Senegalese sole (Solea senegalensis) larvae.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-100">\n        <a href="#cite_note-100">\n         [99]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Ozonate seawater is used for surface disinfection of\n       <a href="/wiki/Haddock" title="Haddock">\n        haddock\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_halibut" title="Atlantic halibut">\n        Atlantic halibut\n       </a>\n       eggs against nodavirus. Nodavirus is a lethal and vertically transmitted virus which causes severe mortality in fish. Haddock eggs should not be treated with high ozone level as eggs so treated did not hatch and died after 3\xe2\x80\x934 days.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-101">\n        <a href="#cite_note-101">\n         [100]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Agriculture">\n        Agriculture\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Ozone&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Agriculture">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Ozone application on freshly cut pineapple and banana shows increase in flavonoids and total phenol contents when exposure is up to 20 minutes. Decrease in\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ascorbic_acid" title="Ascorbic acid">\n        ascorbic acid\n       </a>\n       (one form of\n       <a href="/wiki/Vitamin_C" title="Vitamin C">\n        vitamin C\n       </a>\n       ) content is observed but the positive effect on total phenol content and flavonoids can overcome the negative effect.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-102">\n        <a href="#cite_note-102">\n         [101]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Tomatoes upon treatment with ozone shows an increase in \xce\xb2-carotene, lutein and lycopene.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-103">\n        <a href="#cite_note-103">\n         [102]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       However, ozone application on strawberries in pre-harvest period shows decrease in ascorbic acid content.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-104">\n        <a href="#cite_note-104">\n         [103]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Ozone facilitates the extraction of some heavy metals from soil using\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/EDTA" title="EDTA">\n        EDTA\n       </a>\n       . EDTA forms strong, water-soluble coordination compounds with some heavy metals (\n       <a href="/wiki/Lead" title="Lead">\n        Pb\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Zinc" title="Zinc">\n        Zn\n       </a>\n       ) thereby making it possible to dissolve them out from contaminated soil. If contaminated soil is pre-treated with ozone, the extraction efficacy of\n       <a href="/wiki/Lead" title="Lead">\n        Pb\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Americium" title="Americium">\n        Am\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Plutonium" title="Plutonium">\n        Pu\n       </a>\n       increases by 11.0\xe2\x80\x9328.9%,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-105">\n        <a href="#cite_note-105">\n         [104]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       43.5%\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Plaue_106-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Plaue-106">\n         [105]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and 50.7%\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Plaue_106-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Plaue-106">\n         [105]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       respectively.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Medical">\n        Medical\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Ozone&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Medical">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       See also:\n       <a href="/wiki/Ozone_therapy" title="Ozone therapy">\n        Ozone therapy\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Various therapeutic uses for Ozone have been proposed, but are not supported by peer-reviewed evidence and generally considered\n       <a href="/wiki/Alternative_medicine" title="Alternative medicine">\n        alternative medicine\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ACS_107-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ACS-107">\n         [106]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">\n        See also\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Ozone&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: See also">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Cyclic_ozone" title="Cyclic ozone">\n         Cyclic ozone\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a (GOMOS)\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Global_warming" title="Global warming">\n         Global warming\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Greenhouse_gas" title="Greenhouse gas">\n         Greenhouse gas\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/International_Day_for_the_Preservation_of_the_Ozone_Layer" Action Day\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Ozone_depletion" title="Ozone depletion">\n         Ozone depletion\n        </a>\n        , including the phenomenon known as the ozone hole.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Ozone_therapy" title="Ozone therapy">\n         Ozone therapy\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a class="mw-headline" id="Notes">\n        Notes\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a     </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="reflist" style="list-style-type: lower-alpha;">\n       <div class="mw-references-wrap">\n        <ol class="references">\n         <li id="cite_note-3">\n          <span class="mw-cite-backlink">\n           <b>\n            <a href="#cite_ref-3">\n             ^\n            </a>\n           </b>\n          </span>\n          <span class="reference-text">\n           This vapor pressure is for the\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Critical_temperature" title="Critical temperature">\n            critical temperature\n           </a>\n           , which is below\n           <a href="/wiki/Room_temperature" title="Room temperature">\n            room temperature\n           </a>\n           .\n          </span>\n         </li>\n        </ol>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="References">\n        References\n       </span>\n       <span
